001|# Product Requirement Document: Advanced Tourist Search System
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|
005|**Language**: English (matching user requirements)
006|**Programming Language**: Java (as specified in requirements)
007|**Project Name**: advanced_tourist_search_system
008|**Repository Structure**: 
009|- `/src/main/java/com/tourist/search/` - Main application code
010|- `/src/test/java/com/tourist/search/` - Test cases
011|- `/docs/` - Documentation
012|- `/config/` - Configuration files
013|
014|### Original Requirements Restatement
015|Based on the provided use case, we need to develop an Advanced Search system for tourists that allows authenticated users to:
016|1. Access advanced search functionality from their personal area
017|2. View and fill an advanced search form
018|3. Submit search criteria including location-based parameters
019|4. Receive search results within 15 seconds
020|5. Handle server connection interruptions gracefully
021|
022|## 2. Product Definition
023|
024|### 2.1 Product Goals
025|1. **Enhanced Discovery Experience**: Enable tourists to find relevant sites and attractions through powerful, multi-criteria search capabilities
026|2. **Location-Aware Intelligence**: Leverage tourist location data to provide contextually relevant and personalized search results
027|3. **Performance Optimization**: Ensure all search operations complete within 15 seconds, even with complex queries and large datasets
028|
029|### 2.2 Target Users
030|- **Tourists**: Both domestic and international travelers seeking attractions, accommodations, restaurants, and activities
031|- **Authenticated Users**: Users who have successfully logged into the ETourism system
032|- **Mobile & Desktop Users**: Accessible across different dev
033|
034|## 3. User Stories
035|
036|1. **As an** international tourist visiting a new city, **I want to** filter attractions by category (museums, parks, historical sites), distance from my current location, and opening hours **so that** I can efficiently plan my day and visit relevant sites.
037|2. **As a** budget-conscious traveler, **I want to** search for attractions with specific price ranges, user ratings above 4 stars, and free entry options **so that** I can maximize my experience while staying within budget.
038|3. **As a** family tourist with children, **I want to** filter activities by age-appropriateness, accessibility features (wheelchair access), and family-friendly amenities **so that** I can find suitable attractions for all family members.
039|4. **As a** solo traveler interested in photography, **I want to** search for scenic locations, viewpoints, and photo spots with good lighting conditions and crowd density information **so that** I can capture memorable photographs.

001|# Product Requirement Document: Advanced Tourist Search System
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|
005|**Language**: English (matching user requirements)
006|**Programming Language**: Java (as specified in requirements)
007|**Project Name**: advanced_tourist_search_system
008|**Repository Structure**: 
009|- `/src/main/java/com/tourist/search/` - Main application code
010|- `/src/test/java/com/tourist/search/` - Test cases
011|- `/docs/` - Documentation
012|- `/config/` - Configuration files
013|
014|### Original Requirements Restatement
015|Based on the provided use case, we need to develop an Advanced Search system for tourists that allows authenticated users to:
016|1. Access advanced search functionality from their personal area
017|2. View and fill an advanced search form
018|3. Submit search criteria including location-based parameters
019|4. Receive search results within 15 seconds
020|5. Handle server connection interruptions gracefully
021|
022|## 2. Product Definition
023|
024|### 2.1 Product Goals
025|1. **Enhanced Discovery Experience**: Enable tourists to find relevant sites and attractions through powerful, multi-criteria search capabilities
026|2. **Location-Aware Intelligence**: Leverage tourist location data to provide contextually relevant and personalized search results
027|3. **Performance Optimization**: Ensure all search operations complete within 15 seconds, even with complex queries and large datasets
028|
029|### 2.2 Target Users
030|- **Tourists**: Both domestic and international travelers seeking attractions, accommodations, restaurants, and activities
031|- **Authenticated Users**: Users who have successfully logged into the ETourism system
032|- **Mobile & Desktop Users**: Accessible across different dev
033|
034|## 3. User Stories
035|
036|1. **As an** international tourist visiting a new city, **I want to** filter attractions by category (museums, parks, historical sites), distance from my current location, and opening hours **so that** I can efficiently plan my day and visit relevant sites.
037|2. **As a** budget-conscious traveler, **I want to** search for attractions with specific price ranges, user ratings above 4 stars, and free entry options **so that** I can maximize my experience while staying within budget.
038|3. **As a** family tourist with children, **I want to** filter activities by age-appropriateness, accessibility features (wheelchair access), and family-friendly amenities **so that** I can find suitable attractions for all family members.
039|4. **As a** solo traveler interested in photography, **I want to** search for scenic locations, viewpoints, and photo spots with good lighting conditions and crowd density information **so that** I can capture memorable photographs.
040|5. **As a** tourist with mobility challenges, **I want to** filter attractions by accessibility features, parking availability, and distance from transportation hubs **so that** I can enjoy the destination comfortably.
041|
042|(To be continued with competitive analysis, technical specifications, and requirements pool...)
043|
044|## 4. Competitive Analysis
045|
046|### 4.1 Key Competitors
047|
048|1. **TripAdvisor**
049|   - **Pros**: Massive user base, extensive reviews, comprehensive filtering options, global coverage
050|   - **Cons**: Complex interface, ad-heavy, limited real-time data, performance can be slow
051|
052|2. **Google Maps Tourism Features**
053|   - **Pros**: Excellent location accuracy, real-time data, integration with Google ecosystem
054|   - **Cons**: Limited advanced filtering, basic search capabilities, less focus on tourism-specific needs
055|
056|3. **GetYourGuide**
057|   - **Pros**: Strong focus on tours and activities, booking integration, user-friendly interface
058|   - **Cons**: Limited to bookable experiences, fewer independent attractions, regional coverage gaps
059|
060|4. **Lonely Planet Travel Guides**
061|   - **Pros**: Expert-curated content, detailed destination guides, offline functionality
062|   - **Cons**: Static content, limited real-time updates, minimal user-generated content
063|
064|5. **Booking.com Experiences**
065|   - **Pros**: Strong booking capabilities, integrated with accommodations, user reviews
066|   - **Cons**: Primarily hotel-focused, limited search customization, commission-based model
067|
068|6. **Airbnb Experiences**
069|   - **Pros**: Unique local experiences, strong community aspect, personal hosting
070|   - **Cons**: Limited traditional attractions, quality consistency issues, availability varies
071|
072|7. **Uber Travel**
073|   - **Pros**: Real-time transportation integration, predictive routing, seamless booking
074|   - **Cons**: Limited attraction database, primarily transportation focused, regional availability
075|
076|### 4.2 Competitive Quadrant Chart
077|
078|```mermaid
079|quadrantChart
080|    title "Tourist Search Platforms Competitive Landscape"
081|    x-axis "Limited Search Capabilities" --> "Advanced Search Features"
082|    y-axis "Basic Location Serv" --> "Comprehensive Location Intelligence"
083|    quadrant-1 "Innovation Leaders"
084|    quadrant-2 "Strong Performers"
085|    quadrant-3 "Basic Solutions"
086|    quadrant-4 "Specialized Players"
087|    "TripAdvisor": [0.8, 0.6]
088|    "Google Maps": [0.5, 0.9]
089|    "GetYourGuide": [0.7, 0.4]
090|    "Lonely Planet": [0.3, 0.5]
091|    "Booking.com": [0.4, 0.7]
092|    "Airbnb Experiences": [0.6, 0.3]
093|    "Uber Travel": [0.5, 0.8]
094|    "Our Target Product": [0.9, 0.9]
095|```
096|
097|### 4.3 Market Gaps Identified
098|- **Performance Optimization**: Most platforms struggle with response times for complex queries
099|- **Personalization**: Limited ability to combine multiple user preferences into intelligent recommendations
100|- **Accessibility Focus**: Few platforms offer comprehensive accessibility filtering
101|- **Real-time Data Integration**: Limited integration of live conditions (crowds, weather, events)
102|- **Multi-modal Integration**: Minimal connection between search, booking, and transportation
103|
104|## 5. Technical Specifications
105|
106|### 5.1 Requirements Analysis
107|
108|The system requires a comprehensive solution that includes:
109|1. **Authentication Integration**: Must connect with existing ETourism authentication system
110|2. **Location Serv**: GPS integration for real-time location awareness
111|3. **Advanced Search Engine**: Multi-criteria filtering with complex boolean logic
112|4. **Performance Database**: Optimized for sub-15-second response times
113|5. **Caching Layer**: Intelligent caching to reduce database load
114|6. **Error Handling**: Graceful degradation during server interruptions
115|7. **Mobile Responsiveness**: Support for various device screen sizes
116|
117|### 5.2 Architecture Overview
118|- **Frontend**: Responsive web application (React.js with Material-UI)
119|- **Backend**: Java Spring Boot microserv
120|- **Database**: PostgreSQL with PostGIS for spatial queries
121|- **Cache**: Redis for query results and session storage
122|- **Search Engine**: Elasticsearch for full-text and faceted search
123|- **APIs**: RESTful design with OpenAPI documentation
124|
